There are more than 4.9 million of us of associates who jointly decide the direction of the business and we form a network that supports your prosperity through our financial solutions and we are present in 23 Brazilian states and the federal district with more than 2 thousand branches, distributed in 108 cooperatives. For you to learn about and participate in this transformative movement, we share in this report information on how we generate values ​​with purpose. The main achievements of our Cooperative, the ﬁnancial results, the social results, the events held and the solutions that are at your disposal. Happy reading!2020 ReportEduardo Ferreira President of Sicredi BiomasWe feel victorious upon arriving in 2021 with so many achievements achieved. Perhaps we can say that the greatest of all is satisfaction of our associates, as they are the ones who guide all our actions. It has been 32 years of developing work that seeks to meet the needs of the local reality and, in a sustainable way, contribute to the development of the regions in which we operate. The President's Table and the Cooperative Chat is the moment when we are closest to the members, listening to their needs, always open to suggestions and always willing to adopt measures that will make their daily lives easier. In 2020 we seek alternatives and developed strategies to maintain this contact with members. And then, the President's Table was held in all branches online, reinforcing our commitment to being and always being close to our more than 40 thousand associates, a historic milestone for Sicredi Biomas. Working together for a more prosperous society is our motto. Follow our trajectory over the past year. We feel immensely fulfilled, we hope you are infected by this happiness. Cooperative hug. “The greatest of our achievements is the satisfaction of our associates, as they are the ones who guide all our actions.” Message from the President 4Sicredi Biomas Nossa Cooperativa Sicredi Biomas Nossa Cooperativa surpassed 3 decades of existence in 2019. Today, with 32 years of operation , managing more than 1 billion reais and with more than 40 thousand associates, we are present in 18 municipalities in the states of Mato Grosso and Acre, in addition to consolidating our arrival in Amazonas in 2021. Our annual growth in the last four years reaches an average of 135%. In December, we reached R$1.3 billion in managed resources, a source of great pride and a reflection of confidence. Surpassing the mark of 40 thousand members is a reach that reinforces the trust gained by Sicredi Biomas in the markets where we are present. In this way, we solidify our presence and our commitment to local development and improving quality of life of our members. Currently, Sicredi Biomas is made up of more than 40 thousand members and is present with agencies in 18 municipalities in Mato Grosso and Acre. Araputanga, Mato GrossoHeadquarters of the Cooperative32 years for prosperity: founded on January 29, 1989, the Sicredi Biomas cooperative In 2009, members approved the change of name to Free Admission Credit Cooperative for Members of the Northwest of MT. In 2015, after approval at the assembly, the cooperative began the expansion process for Acre. In 2020, expansion to the state of Amazonas was approved, changing its name to Sicredi Biomas MT AC AM. 5MT AC AM, began its activities in Araputanga with the 23 founding partners, still under the name of Rural Credit Cooperative of the Northwest of Mato Grosso - Credinoroeste. The Cooperative was created to support small rural producers in the region. Nucleus Coordinators Reception of associates at a nucleus assembly Reserva do Cabaçal, MTR2020 ReportSicredi Biomas13Assemblies In the photo, Ediano José Neves, Executive Director of Sicredi Biomas, talks about the topic of Allocation of Cooperative Results to members in the city of Araputanga, MT. As happens annually, in the first semester of January, Sicredi Biomas carries out the process of accountability to members and deliberations on the direction of the Cooperative. In 2020, 19 Core Assemblies were held, one for each agency. The events took place in person in each of the 18 cities in Mato Grosso and Acre. The presentations were led by the executive director, Ediano José Neves, the operations director, Luciano Pereira de Andrade, and the regional managers Ricardo Medeiros and Ueligton Júlio and the manager of each agency. In addition to presenting the results for 2019, such as credit operations, assets and equity, and the objectives for 2020, the meetings defined the allocation of results and resources from Fates, the Social Fund and the Expansion Fund. Furthermore, in Indiavaí there was an election of Center Coordinators.Report 2020Pertencer Program Renewing and bringing new knowledge about cooperativism is a concern that Sicredi Biomas has for the community. This commitment extends to our core coordinators. To ensure the success and longevity of a cooperative, the participation of members in its management and development is essential. Monitor and supervise the actions of managers, whether through participation in meetings and assemblies or through the actions of Administration and Fiscal advisors and core coordinators elected by members. This is all part of governance practices, constituting a right and a duty of the member. The training of core coordinators was carried out in a modular way. There were six face-to-face meetings, which started in 2018 and the last stage of these meetings took place in January 2020. As a way of closing this training cycle, the next step will be a trip to all coordinators who participated in at least 75% of the in-person training, the trip will be an institutional visit to Rio Grande do Sul, promoting a tourist tour and getting to know the Cooperativism Route. The nucleus coordinators were elected by the members during the assembly process. For the president of the Cooperative, Eduardo Ferreira, the more qualified the members are, the better the management of the Cooperative will be. “We want to reinforce and promote the principles of cooperativism so that our core coordinators can contribute to the improvement of our cooperative. We want to do shared management, so that together we can have good results.” 14Sicredi Biomas152018 1,522 2019 2,563 2020 2,998Crescer Program In order to spread the culture of cooperativism and credit cooperatives among our members, we developed the Crescer Program. Through it, we offer training that expands understanding of how a society works cooperative and the role of the member in the governance of a cooperative business, helping to form new leaders. In 2020, Sicredi Biomas created strategies to overcome the barriers imposed by the pandemic and thus developing ways to bring cooperative knowledge to everyone. Opportunities were generated through online training or even individual training for members to better understand the cooperative business model. Graduates of the Crescermovimento Program are carried out in the Welcome modules, where new members receive basic information about the differences between cooperative and banking ﬁnancial institutions, and in the Crescer Program meetings, a face-to-face module that brings together members for a more in-depth conversation about the characteristics of the cooperative enterprise. The Crescer Program directly follows the lives of members after training and provides information that shows the transparency of the business model, which further proves the credibility and transparency of the Cooperative. So for us, especially in the interior of the country, the first two months were filled with training and face-to-face actions. Our planning In-person training took place with employees from across the Cooperative, including those from Acre. Meetings by segment took place in the first three weeks of the second month of 2020, bringing together employees from the Agro, Individual and Legal Entities segments in the events Entressafra de Ideias, Workshop PF Investimentos and Workplay, respectively. Attentive to the needs of the communities where it operates, Sicredi Biomas has contributed to preventing coronavirus on several fronts. “As a Cooperative Financial Institution, we understand that the best actions are those that bring results for everyone. Therefore, we are encouraged to make our contribution with actions that seek to protect people, both in terms of health and the economy”, highlights Ediano Neves, executive director of the Cooperative. In addition to the allocation of financial resources to hospital institutions and NGOs, the The cooperative has prioritized care in protecting members and employees, encouraging the use of digital channels, reducing circulation at service agencies, promoting virtual meetings and adopting home office. With the lockdown decrees and distancing guidelines from the Ministries of Health, as well as the safety guidelines from the World Health Organization, a general alignment was carried out with all employees. Ways to maintain a close relationship even with closed agencies and observing the distance between people, were debated in this live and the ideas became a set of good practice actions that we have exercised until then in our daily lives. In order to know the personal, professional and of our associates, our more than 300 employees seek to be present in their daily lives, cultivating an increasingly close relationship. As they are also members of the Cooperative, they participate of decisions that impact their management and are engaged in the prosperity of the business and supported projects. Throughout 2020, a series of training and online events were held with the aim of preparing our employees to serve their members even better. In the reality we were in, the uncertainties generated a need for alignment among all employees, ensuring their health and minimizing the health risks of our associates 19Sicredi BiomasPessoas impacted by financial education initiatives 2018 722 2019 1955 2020 11,578Financial Education At Sicredi Biomas, we believe that we have a responsibility to support our associates in managing their personal finances and in the conscious use of our products and services. That's why we have initiatives aimed at financial education. Sicredi's main systemic action on this topic is ENEF Week, an initiative by CONEF (National Financial Education Committee) to promote National Financial Education Strategy. Organized by the Central Bank of Brazil between the 20th and 26th of May 2020, it included the participation of financial organizations from across the country, who carried out free educational actions to publicize the topic. Online financial education lecture Sicredi Biomas 20Report 202021Communities R$ 14 million R$ 353 thousand The work of our Cooperative consists of raising resources from members and lending them to other members in the same region, creating a support network that stimulates the prosperity of everyone involved and positively impacts the places where we operate. Through our products and services, we promote the financial inclusion of the population and boost the local economy. As a result, we help improve the quality of life for our associates, their families and communities. We also have a series of private social investment actions, which seek to meet local needs and strengthen community relations. This way, the more our Cooperative grows and prospers, the greater our positive impact. We call this process of joint development of the Cooperative, the member and the community Sicredi Virtuoso Cycle. And next Saturday (04.07), cooperatives across the country, including Sicredi, celebrate the day of one of the largest volunteer programs in Brazil, called Cooperate Day (C Day), always celebrated on the first Saturday in July. Promoted by the Organization of Brazilian Cooperatives (OCB), the date is a celebration of International Cooperative Day, with activities carried out by volunteers in the areas of health, leisure, education and the environment to transform realities. Since the year Last year, the concept of the program changed and, instead of the actions being concentrated on a single date, they began to be carried out throughout the year. Dia C Jauru, MTOther programs and initiatives The Sicredi Social Fund aims to support entities, activities or projects that, due to the value received, generate benefits and improvements for people living in the communities where the cooperative financial institution is present, highlighting Sicredi's Corporate Citizenship causes, which are Cooperation, Education and Local Development.Sicredi Biomas 23Eco-efficiency In order to reduce our impact on the environment and increase the generation of value for the communities where we are present, we seek to make agencies of our cooperative as a whole, more sustainable in their operations. In 2020, Sicredi Biomas continued and reinforced a destination project of recyclable solid waste that began in 2019. The project started at the Cooperative Headquarters had a local partnership with the Reciclar para Viver Melhor Association of Collectors and for greater commitment from the entire internal team, communication was developed at the headquarters and the acquisition of bins for the materials recyclable materials, in addition to the engagement promoted by the team. The proposal is to extend the project to surrounding cities and subsequently to those cities that have infrastructure that allows reuse of recyclable materials. Therefore, we intend to surpass the neutralization mark of 955.64t of CO2 in 2019, equivalent through carbon credits certiﬁed by the Veriﬁed Carbon Standard seal for 2019. As a result of this initiative, in 2020 we stopped sending more than 90 % of materials in addition to supporting the collectors' association and making employees aware of the importance of selective collection. 242020 ReportOur Associated Results (thousands) Credit (millions of R$) Deposits (millions of R$) Savings (millions of R$) Assets (billions of R$) Net Worth (millions of R$) 2018 31,371 2019 35,076 2020 40,748 2018 564.2 2019 778.0 2020 927.9 2018 347.7 2019 451.5 2020 694.3 2018 152.2 2019 166.9 2020 255.7 2018 0.7 2019 1.0 2020 1.3 2018 131 2019 157 2020 199 Main numbers in the decade Associates (thousands) 40,748 Assets under management (billions) 1.3 Net worth (millions) 199 1.03 Credit operations (billions) Associates (thousand) 15,264 Managed assets (billions) 0.1 Shareholders' equity (millions) 17 0.08Credit operations (billions)2010 20202020 Report 2526São José dos Quatro MarcosNew PF Platform Lambari d'OesteAraputanga, MTProjeto Mais Leite Novo Caixa Digital transformation In the month of July, from the 6th to the 10th, content relevant to agribusiness in the state and the world was covered for an hour every day, such as: opportunities in agriculture, a look at agriculture family, changes to the harvest plan, rural credit in practice and deﬁning the next steps on how to act with credit in the region in light of the scenario for 2020 and 2021. Our agricultural actions in 2020 established solid partnerships. The Mais Leite project was a partnership with the lacbom dairy and the Rabobank foundation. Among the project's objectives are increased dairy productivity, rational use of land and water, construction of manure pits, improvement of milk quality, acquisition and modernization. dog of equipment, sustainability with genetic improvement of the herd and technical assistance from technical professionals from Coope-noroeste. The project is being carried out with 10 milk producers in Araputanga, all family farmers, most of whom have never taken out credit. The project is an international partnership model that Sicredi seeks to build to facilitate rural producers’ access to credit. Since 2018, digital transformation has already been a reality in our country Cooperative with delivery of Woop Sicredi to our digital account. Much more than changing our systems, Digital transformation is a change in the way we operate and in the experience with our members, after all, no matter how innovative the technology is, the user is always at the center of our attention. Improve our processes and give more autonomy to our associates and collaborators. In our opinion, the financial statements referred to above adequately present, in all material respects, the equity and financial position of the Cooperativa de Cré said, Poupança e Investment of the Northwest of Mato Grosso, Acre and Amazonas - Sicredi Biomas on December 31, 2020, the performance of its operations and its cash flows for the year ended on that date, in accordance with the accounting practices adopted in Brazil applicable to institutions authorized to operate by the Central Bank of Brazil (BACEN), including Resolution No. 4, 818 of May 29, 2020 of the National Monetary Council (CMN) and BCB Resolution No. 2 of August 12, 2020 of BACEN. Basis for opinion Our audit was conducted in accordance with Brazilian and international auditing standards. Our responsibilities, in accordance with such standards, are described in the following section entitled “Auditor's responsibilities for the audit of financial statements”. We are independent in relation to the Cooperative, in accordance with the relevant ethical principles set out in the Accountant's Code of Professional Ethics and in the professional standards issued by the Federal Accounting Council, and we comply with other ethical responsibilities in accordance with these standards. We believe that the audit evidence obtained is sufficient and appropriate to support our opinion. Other information accompanying the financial statements and the auditor's report The management of the Cooperative is responsible for this other information that comprises the management report. Our opinion on the financial statements does not cover the management report and we do not express any form of audit conclusion on that report. 2 In connection with the audit of the financial statements, our responsibility is to read the management report and, in doing so, consider whether that report is materially inconsistent with the financial statements or with our knowledge obtained in the audit or otherwise appears to be materially distorted. If, based on the work carried out, if we conclude that there is a material misstatement in the management report, we are required to communicate this fact. We have nothing to report in this regard. Management and governance responsibilities for the financial statements Management is responsible for the preparation and adequate presentation of the financial statements in accordance with the accounting practices adopted in Brazil, applicable to institutions authorized to operate by the Bank Central do Brasil, including Resolution No. 4,818/20 of the National Monetary Council (CMN) and Resolution No. 02/20 of the Central Bank of Brazil (BACEN) and for the internal controls that it determined as necessary to allow the preparation of financial statements free from material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or error. When preparing the financial statements, management is responsible for assessing the Cooperative's ability to continue operating, disclosing, when applicable, matters related to its operational continuity and the use of this accounting basis in the preparation of financial statements unless management intends to liquidate the Cooperative or cease its operations, or has no realistic alternative to avoid closure of operations. Those responsible for the Cooperative's governance are those responsible for supervising the process of preparing the financial statements. Auditor's responsibilities for auditing the financial statements Our objectives are to obtain reasonable assurance that the financial statements, taken as a whole, are free from material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or error, and to issue an audit report containing our opinion. Reasonable security is a high level of security, but not a guarantee that the audit performed, in accordance with Brazilian and international auditing standards, always detects any relevant distortions that may exist. Distortions may result from fraud and/or error and are considered material when, individually or together, they may influence, within a reasonable perspective, the economic decisions of users taken based on the aforementioned financial statements. As part of the audit carried out, in accordance with Brazilian and international auditing standards, we exercise professional judgment and maintain professional skepticism throughout the audit. In addition:  We identify and assess the risks of material misstatement in the financial statements, whether caused by fraud or error, plan and perform audit procedures in response to such risks, and obtain sufficient appropriate audit evidence to support our opinion . The risk of not detecting a material misstatement resulting from fraud is greater than that arising from error, since the Fraud may involve the act of circumventing internal controls, collusion, forgery, omission or intentional misrepresentations.  We have obtained an understanding of the internal controls relevant to the audit to plan audit procedures appropriate to the circumstances, but not for the purpose of expressing an opinion on the effectiveness of the Cooperative's internal controls. A member company of Ernst & Young Global Limited 3  We assess the suitability of accounting policies used and the reasonableness of accounting estimates and respective disclosures made by management.  We conclude on the appropriateness of management's use of the going concern basis of accounting and, based on the audit evidence obtained, whether there is material uncertainty regarding events or conditions that may raise significant doubt regarding the ability to continue as a going concern operational of the Cooperative. If we conclude that there is material uncertainty, we should draw attention in our audit report to the related disclosures in the financial statements or include a modification to our opinion if the disclosures are inadequate. Our conclusions are based on audit evidence obtained up to the date of our report. However, future events or conditions may lead the Cooperative to no longer maintain operational continuity.  We evaluate the general presentation, structure and content of the financial statements, including disclosures and whether the financial statements represent the corresponding transactions and events in a manner compatible with the objective of fair presentation. We communicate with those charged with governance regarding, among other things, the scope and timing of planned audit engagements and significant audit findings, including significant deficiencies in internal controls that may have been identified during our work. As members of the Fiscal Council of the Credit, Savings Cooperative eInvestimento do Noroeste de Mato Grosso, Acre eAmazonas -Sicredi Biomas and in the exercise of legal and statutory powers, we examine the Administration Report and the Financial Statements comprising: Balance Sheet, Statement of Surplus or Losses, Statement of Changes in Net Equity, Statement of Cash Flows, Explanatory Notes and additional statements, and respective audit report on the financial statements, documents relating to the year ended in December 31, 2020. Due to the Governance policies adopted by the Cooperative and based on our examinations and the independent auditors' audit report, issued by Ernst & Young Auditores Independentes S.S., we are in favor of approving the aforementioned statements.
